data-v-11a5842c="" data-v-d13d8f28="" class="card v1"><div data-v-11a5842c="" class="card__content"><div data-v-fa79d6d9="" data-v-d13d8f28="" class="loading"><div data-v-fa79d6d9="" class="loading__img"></div><div data-v-fa79d6d9="" class="loading__content"><div data-v-d13d8f28="" class="news-detail" data-section-name="Contents" data-section-number="2"><div data-v-d13d8f28="" class="news-detail__little-info"><div data-v-d13d8f28="" class="news-detail__news-type update">update</div><div data-v-d13d8f28="" class="news-detail__live-date">2 Oct 2024</div></div><h1 data-v-d13d8f28="" class="news-detail__title title xs">v.254 - Midnight Carnival - Ludibrium Update Preview</h1><div data-v-51464747="" data-v-d13d8f28="" class="cms-html-wrapper"><div style="background-color: #1f1e57; color: #ffffff; text-align: center;">
<p><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/ku1h1whl/keyart.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-left: 5%; padding-right: 5%; text-align: center;"><strong>BOO!</strong> Our <strong>Night Troupe</strong> is making its daring return just in time for the mischievous season of Halloween! We have lots in store to really get this season going! You can start with earning bonus stats by leveling up your <strong>Festival Designer Rank</strong> in Ludibrium or you can kick back and put together some solid fits through our <strong>Maple Fashion Week</strong>. Is dressing yourself up not enough?! That’s fine! You can put your interior design skills to the test by decorating your space through the <strong>[Home] Halloween</strong> event!</p>
<p style="padding-top: 2%; padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/umvlu0hc/night-troupe-header.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-left: 5%; padding-right: 5%; text-align: center;">We’ve been to Henesys, Rien, Nautilus... and now, it’s time to explore the castle of toys! The <strong>Night Troupe</strong> is back and this time, they’re taking us to <strong>Ludibrium</strong>!</p>
<p style="padding-left: 5%; padding-right: 5%; text-align: center;">Level up your <strong>Festival Designer Rank</strong> to unlock bonus stats, and power up even more with <strong>Festival Decorating</strong> perks that give your character (and boss mules) extra gains! Time doesn’t play by the rules here! Choose to fill either the <strong>Eos Hourglass</strong> or the <strong>Helios Hourglass</strong> and enjoy a boost in EXP - past, present, or future, the choice is yours.</p>
<p style="padding-top: 2%; padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/ck5htp4g/night-troupe-ss.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-left: 5%; padding-right: 5%; text-align: center;">Need a break after all that grinding? Grab your friends and enjoy the <strong>Ludibrium Fireworks Display</strong>, then jump right back in for a fun challenge - <strong>Knocking Down Blockulatus</strong>!</p>
<p style="padding-top: 2%; padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/452jf4rw/maple-fashion-week-header.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-left: 5%; padding-right: 5%; text-align: center;">FashionStory IS the true endgame! Get ready, because <strong>Hallowkitty</strong> and <strong>Camila</strong> are back and thrilled to host <strong>Maple Fashion Week</strong>! Defeat enemies to unlock your next outfit of the day and show off your style down the runway.</p>
<p style="padding-top: 2%; padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/0w1jxqsd/maple-fashion-week-art.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/rhqbbodd/halloween-header.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-left: 5%; padding-right: 5%; text-align: center;">Your Maple World neighbors have no idea what Halloween is really about, so it’s time to team up with Querencia and show them what it’s all about… and maybe give them a little scare! Get creative and decorate your own <strong>Halloween Manor</strong> to really set the mood for the perfect fright night!</p>
<p style="padding-top: 2%; padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/saapfcup/halloween-ss.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/phshtggp/legion-relay-header.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-left: 5%; padding-right: 5%; text-align: center;">Race to the finish line in the <strong>Legion Relay</strong>! Earn daily quests and earn rewards to supercharge your Legion! There are three types of <strong>Relay Box Rewards</strong> to choose from, all offering the same rewards but in different quantities. The higher the quantity of the reward, the lower the chance of obtaining it. Choose wisely!</p>
<p style="padding-top: 2%; padding-bottom: 2%;"><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/0rynl3pn/legion-relay-ss.png" alt=""></p>
<p><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/tsqbcgim/sunny-sunday.png" alt=""></p>
<p style="padding-top: 2%; padding-bottom: 2%;"><a href="https://forums.maplestory.nexon.net/"><img style="padding-right: 2%;" src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/zaqi32t4/discuss-on-forums.png" alt=""></a><a href="https://discord.gg/maplestory"><img style="padding-left: 2%;" src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/d1pdk3yi/discuss-on-discord.png" alt=""></a></p>
<p><img src="//g.nexonstatic.com/media/p0pb43xb/footer.png" alt=""></p>
